Say your company name and what services you offer. You can also say beautify to enhance your description.\");\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1000);\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (SR) {\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n      \n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; With years of experience and a commitment to quality, we deliver exceptional results on every project.`;\n      await typeIntoField('builder-profile-textarea', enhanced, 'Profile', setLocalProfile, onChange);\n      speak(\"Description enhanced!\");\n    } finally {\n      setIsBeautifying(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const processVoice = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    // Beautify command\n    if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance') || lower.includes('improve')) {\n      handleBeautify();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Extract company name\n    const companyPatterns = [\n      /(?:my company is|company name is|we are|i'm from|this is)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\s+and|\\s+we|\\.|$)/i,\n      /^(.+?)\\s+(?:construction|builders|contracting|development)/i\n    ];\n    \n    for (const pattern of companyPatterns) {\n      const match = text.match(pattern);\n      if (match && match[1]) {\n        await typeIntoField('builder-company-input', match[1].trim(), 'Company Name', setLocalCompany, onCompanyChange);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Extract services/description\n    const servicePatterns = [\n      /(?:we offer|we do|we specialize in|services include|we build)\\s+(.+)/i,\n      /(?:and we|we also)\\s+(.+)/i\n    ];\n    \n    for (const pattern of servicePatterns) {\n      const match = text.match(pattern);\n      if (match && match[1]) {\n        await typeIntoField('builder-profile-textarea', match[1].trim(), 'Services', setLocalProfile, onChange);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Commands\n    if (lower.includes('save') || lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue')) {\n      if (localCompany.trim() && localProfile.trim()) onSave();\n    }\n  }, [localCompany, localProfile, onCompanyChange, onChange, onSave]);\n\n  const toggleListening = () => {\n    if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); Our dedicated team provides personalized service to help clients achieve their real estate goals.`;\n      await typeIntoField('agent-profile-textarea', enhanced, 'Profile', setLocalProfile, onChange);\n      speak(\"Profile enhanced!\");\n    } finally {\n      setIsBeautifying(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const processVoice = async (text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance')) { handleBeautify(); WalkingCursor from '../common/WalkingCursor';\n\ninterface Props { onClose: () => void; onBack: () => void; }\n\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'preferences' | 'complete';\nconst STEPS: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'preferences', 'complete'];\nconst LABELS = ['Phone', 'Verify', 'Preferences', 'Done'];\nconst THEME = { primary: '#0f172a', secondary: '#1e293b', accent: '#06b6d4' };\n\nconst CATEGORIES = ['Flooring', 'Lighting', 'Kitchen', 'Bathroom', 'Outdoor', 'Smart Home', 'Furniture', 'Decor'];\n\nconst CustomerFlow: React.FC<Props> = ({ onClose, onBack }) => {\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\n  const [selectedCategories, setSelectedCategories] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [walkerActive, setWalkerActive] = useState(true);\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n\n  const synth = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\n  const speak = useCallback((t: string) => { synth?.cancel(); const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(t); u.rate = 0.95; synth?.speak(u); }, [synth]);\n\n  const goNext = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i < STEPS.length - 1) { setStep(STEPS[i + 1]); setWalkerActive(true); } };\n  const goBack = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i > 0) setStep(STEPS[i - 1]); else onBack(); };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const messages: Record<Step, string> = {\n      phone: \"Welcome customer! Enter your phone number to get started.\",\n      otp: \"Enter the verification code.\",\n      preferences: \"Select your interests. Say the category name to toggle.\",\n      complete: \"You're all set!\"\n    };\n    speak(messages[step]);\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1000);\n  }, [step]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (SR) {\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        setTranscript(text);\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) processVoice(text);\n      };\n      recognitionRef.current.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\n      recognitionRef.current.onend = () => { if (isListening) recognitionRef.current?.start(); };\n    }\n    return () => recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n  }, [isListening, step, selectedCategories]);\n\n  const startListening = () => { try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); setIsListening(true); } catch (e) {} };\n  const toggleListening = () => { if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); setIsListening(false); } else { startListening(); } };\n\n  const processVoice = async (text: string) => {\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0' };\n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\b${word}\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length > 0) {\n      const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n      setPhone(newPhone);\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) speak(\"Phone complete!\");\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\n      setOtp(newOtp);\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) speak(\"Code complete!\");\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'preferences') {\n      CATEGORIES.forEach(cat => {\n        if (lower.includes(cat.toLowerCase())) {\n          setSelectedCategories(prev => {\n            if (prev.includes(cat)) {\n              speak(`Removed ${cat}`);\n              return prev.filter(c => c !== cat);\n            } else {\n              speak(`Added ${cat}`);\n              return [...prev, cat];\n            }\n          });\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue') || lower.includes('done')) {\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) goNext();\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) goNext();\n      else if (step === 'preferences') goNext();\n    }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => { if (p.length <= 3) return p; if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`; return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`; };\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  const AgenticBar = () => (\n    <div style={{ marginTop: 20, padding: 16, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 16, border: `2px solid ${isListening ? STEPS: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'preferences', 'complete'];\\nconst LABELS = ['Phone', 'Verify', 'Preferences', 'Done'];\\nconst THEME = { primary: '#0f172a', secondary: '#1e293b', accent: '#06b6d4' };\\n\\nconst CATEGORIES = ['Flooring', 'Lighting', 'Kitchen', 'Bathroom', 'Outdoor', 'Smart Home', 'Furniture', 'Decor'];\\n\\nconst CustomerFlow: React.FC<Props> = ({ onClose, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\\n  const [selectedCategories, setSelectedCategories] = useState<string[]>([]);\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [walkerActive, setWalkerActive] = useState(true);\\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\\n\\n  const synth = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\\n  const speak = useCallback((t: string) => { synth?.cancel(); const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(t); u.rate = 0.95; synth?.speak(u); }, [synth]);\\n\\n  const goNext = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i < STEPS.length - 1) { setStep(STEPS[i + 1]); setWalkerActive(true); } };\\n  const goBack = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i > 0) setStep(STEPS[i - 1]); else onBack(); };\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const messages: Record<Step, string> = {\\n      phone: \\\"Welcome customer! Enter your phone number to get started.\\\",\\n      otp: \\\"Enter the verification code.\\\",\\n      preferences: \\\"Select your interests. Say the category name to toggle.\\\",\\n      complete: \\\"You're all set!\\\"\\n    };\\n    speak(messages[step]);\\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1000);\\n  }, [step]);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (SR) {\\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n        let text = '';\\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) processVoice(text);\\n      };\\n      recognitionRef.current.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\\n      recognitionRef.current.onend = () => { if (isListening) recognitionRef.current?.start(); };\\n    }\\n    return () => recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n  }, [isListening, step, selectedCategories]);\\n\\n  const startListening = () => { try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); setIsListening(true); } catch (e) {} };\\n  const toggleListening = () => { if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); setIsListening(false); } else { startListening(); } };\\n\\n  const processVoice = async (text: string) => {\\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0' };\\n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\\\\\b${word}\\\\\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\\n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n\\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n      setPhone(newPhone);\\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) speak(\\\"Phone complete!\\\");\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\\n      setOtp(newOtp);\\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) speak(\\\"Code complete!\\\");\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'preferences') {\\n      CATEGORIES.forEach(cat => {\\n        if (lower.includes(cat.toLowerCase())) {\\n          setSelectedCategories(prev => {\\n            if (prev.includes(cat)) {\\n              speak(`Removed ${cat}`);\\n              return prev.filter(c => c !== cat);\\n            } else {\\n              speak(`Added ${cat}`);\\n              return [...prev, cat];\\n            }\\n          });\\n        }\\n      });\\n    }\\n\\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue') || lower.includes('done')) {\\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) goNext();\\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) goNext();\\n      else if (step === 'preferences') goNext();\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => { if (p.length <= 3) return p; if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`; return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`; };\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n\\n  const AgenticBar = () => (\\n    <div style={{ marginTop: 20, padding: 16, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 16, border: `2px solid ${isListening ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}` }}>\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\\n        <div style={{ width: 10, height: 10, borderRadius: '50%', background: isListening ? '#10b981' : '#64748b', animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none' }} />\\n        <span style={{ color: '#06b6d4', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\ud83c\\udfa4 {isListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'READY'}</span>\\n      </div>\\n      {isListening && (<div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 3, height: 25, alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 10 }}>{[...Array(12)].map((_, i) => (<div key={i} style={{ width: 3, background: 'linear-gradient(to top, #10b981, #06b6d4)', borderRadius: 2, animation: `wave 0.4s ease-in-out ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`, height: 8 }} />))}</div>)}\\n      {transcript && (<div style={{ background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 8, padding: '10px 14px', marginBottom: 12 }}><p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', margin: 0 }}>\\\"{transcript}\\\"</p></div>)}\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\\n        <button onClick={toggleListening} style={{ padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: 25, border: 'none', background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : '#10b981', color: 'white', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer' }}>{isListening ? ref.current.focus();\n    ref.current.classList.add('vv-filling');\n    for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));\n      const newValue = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i > 0) setStep(STEPS[i - 1]); else onBack(); };\n\n  const typeIntoField = async (ref: React.RefObject<HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement>, value: string, setter: (v: = value.substring(0, i);\n      setter(value.substring(0, i));\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0' };\n    let We provide expert guidance to help clients achieve their real estate goals.`;\n      await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, enhanced, setDescription);\n    }\n    setIsBeautifying(false);\n    speak('Enhanced!');\n  };\n\n  const saveAgent = async () => {\n    try {\n      await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/agents', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ phone, license, licenseState, companyName, description, files: uploadedFiles })\n      });\n    } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => { if (p.length <= 3) return p; if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`; return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`; };\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  const getWelcome = () => {\n    switch (step) {\n      case 'phone': return 'Welcome real estate agent! ]\\n};\\n\\nconst MultiFormatUploader: React.FC<MultiFormatUploaderProps> = ({\\n  onFilesUploaded,\\n  onAllComplete,\\n  speak,\\n  userType,\\n  accentColor = '#10b981'\\n}) => {\\n  const STEP 4: Fix VendorFlow with working AgenticBar\\n#\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\u2550\\necho \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udce6 Fixing VendorFlow...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$VENDOR_DIR/VendorFlow.tsx\\\" << 'VENDORFLOW'\\nimport React, { useState, useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from => void;\\n  onBack: () => void;\\n}\\n\\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'profile' | 'upload' | 'complete';\\nconst STEPS: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'profile', 'upload', 'complete'];\\nconst LABELS = {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\\n  const [companyName, setCompanyName] = useState('');\\n  const [description, setDescription] = useState('');\\n  const [isBeautifying, setIsBeautifying] = useState(false);\\n  const [uploadedFiles, setUploadedFiles] = useState<any[]>([]);\\n  \\n  const []);\\n\\n  const goNext = () => {\\n    const i = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n    if (i < STEPS.length - 1) {\\n      setStep(STEPS[i + 1]);\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const goBack = () => {\\n    const i = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n    if (i > 0) {\\n      setStep(STEPS[i - 1]);\\n    } else {\\n      onBack();\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  // Auto-fill with typewriter effect\\n  const typeIntoField = async (ref: React.RefObject<HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement>, value: string, setter: (v: string) => void) => {\\n    if (!ref.current) return;\\n    \\n    ref.current.focus();\\n    ref.current.classList.add('vv-filling');\\n    \\n    for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));\\n      const newValue = value.substring(0, i);\\n      ref.current.value = newValue;\\n      setter(newValue);\\n    }\\n    \\n    ref.current.classList.remove('vv-filling');\\n    ref.current.classList.add('vv-filled');\\n    setTimeout(() => ref.current?.classList.remove('vv-filled'), 500);\\n  };\\n\\n  // Process voice commands\\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    console.log('Processing command:', text);\\n\\n    // Number conversion\\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = {\\n      'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4',\\n      'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0'\\n    };\\n    \\n    let processed = lower;\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Phone step\\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n      await typeIntoField(phoneInputRef, newPhone, setPhone);\\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) {\\n        speak('Phone number complete! Say next or click Send OTP.');\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // OTP step\\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\\n      await typeIntoField(otpInputRef, newOtp, setOtp);\\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) {\\n        speak('Code complete! Say verify or click the button.');\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Profile step - Company name extraction\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\n      const companyPatterns = [\\n        /(?:my company is|company name is|we are|i'm from|this is|called)\\\\s+(.+?)(?:\\\\s+and|\\\\s+we|\\\\.|$)/i,\\n        /^(.+?)\\\\s+(?:inc|llc|corp|company|co\\\\b)/i\\n      ];\\n      \\n      for (const pattern of companyPatterns) {\\n        const match = text.match(pattern);\\n        if (match && match[1] && match[1].length > 2) {\\n          await typeIntoField(companyInputRef, match[1].trim(), setCompanyName);\\n          speak(`Got it, ${match[1].trim()}.`);\\n          break;\\n        }\\n      }\\n\\n      // Description extraction\\n      const descPatterns = [\\n        /(?:we sell|we offer|we make|we provide|we specialize in|dealing in)\\\\s+(.+)/i,\\n        /(?:our products include|products are|selling)\\\\s+(.+)/i\\n      ];\\n      \\n      for (const pattern of descPatterns) {\\n        const match = text.match(pattern);\\n        if (match && match[1]) {\\n          await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, match[1].trim(), setDescription);\\n          break;\\n        }\\n      }\\n\\n      // Beautify command\\n      if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance') || lower.includes('improve')) {\\n        handleBeautify();\\n      }\\n    }\\n\\n    // Navigation commands\\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue') || lower.includes('send') || lower.includes('verify') || lower.includes('save')) {\\n      if (step === 'phone' && onBack(); };\\n\\n  const typeIntoField = async (ref: React.RefObject<HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement>, value: string, setter: (v: string) => void) => {\\n    if (!ref.current) return;\\n    ref.current.focus();\\n    ref.current.classList.add('vv-filling');\\n    for (let i = 0; i <= value.length; i++) {\\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 50));\\n      const newValue = value.substring(0, i);\\n      ref.current.value = newValue;\\n      setter(newValue);\\n    }\\n    ref.current.classList.remove('vv-filling');\\n  };\\n\\n  const handleVoiceCommand = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0' };\\n    let processed = lower;\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) processed = 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\\n      await typeIntoField(otpInputRef, newOtp, setOtp);\\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) speak('Code complete!');\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'profile') {\\n      const companyMatch = text.match(/(?:company is|called|we are|i'm from)\\\\s+(.+?)(?:\\\\s+and|\\\\.|$)/i);\\n      if (companyMatch && companyMatch[1]) if (descMatch && descMatch[1]) await typeIntoField(descriptionRef, descMatch[1].trim(), setDescription);\\n      \\n      if (lower.includes('beautify')) handleBeautify();\\n    }\\n\\n    if
